#
# $pkg_postinst_busybox
#   rename from pkg_postinst_${PN} data.py:170 [expandKeys]
#     "	# This part of code is dedicated to the on target upgrade problem.
#     	# It's known that if we don't make appropriate symlinks before update-alternatives calls,
#     	# there will be errors indicating missing commands such as 'sed'.
#     	# These symlinks will later be updated by update-alternatives calls.
#     	test -n 2 > /dev/null || alias test='busybox test'
#     	if test "x$D" = "x"; then
#     		# Remove busybox.nosuid if it's a symlink, because this situation indicates
#     		# that we're installing or upgrading to a one-binary busybox.
#     		if test -h /bin/busybox.nosuid; then
#     			rm -f /bin/busybox.nosuid
#     		fi
#     		for suffix in "" ".nosuid" ".suid"; do
#     			if test -e /etc/busybox.links$suffix; then
#     				while read link; do
#     					if test ! -e "$link"; then
#     						case "$link" in
#     							/*/*/*)
#     								to="../../bin/busybox$suffix"
#     								;;
#     							/bin/*)
#     								to="busybox$suffix"
#     								;;
#     							/*/*)
#     								to="../bin/busybox$suffix"
#     								;;
#     						esac
#     						# we can use busybox here because even if we are using splitted busybox
#     						# we've made a symlink from /bin/busybox to /bin/busybox.nosuid.
#     						busybox rm -f $link
#     						busybox ln -s $to $link
#     					fi
#     				done < /etc/busybox.links$suffix
#     			fi
#     		done
#     	fi
#     "
pkg_postinst_busybox="	# This part of code is dedicated to the on target upgrade problem. \
	# It's known that if we don't make appropriate symlinks before update-alternatives calls, \
	# there will be errors indicating missing commands such as 'sed'. \
	# These symlinks will later be updated by update-alternatives calls. \
	test -n 2 > /dev/null || alias test='busybox test' \
	if test \"x$D\" = \"x\"; then \
		# Remove busybox.nosuid if it's a symlink, because this situation indicates \
		# that we're installing or upgrading to a one-binary busybox. \
		if test -h /bin/busybox.nosuid; then \
			rm -f /bin/busybox.nosuid \
		fi \
		for suffix in \"\" \".nosuid\" \".suid\"; do \
			if test -e /etc/busybox.links$suffix; then \
				while read link; do \
					if test ! -e \"$link\"; then \
						case \"$link\" in \
							/*/*/*) \
								to=\"../../bin/busybox$suffix\" \
								;; \
							/bin/*) \
								to=\"busybox$suffix\" \
								;; \
							/*/*) \
								to=\"../bin/busybox$suffix\" \
								;; \
						esac \
						# we can use busybox here because even if we are using splitted busybox \
						# we've made a symlink from /bin/busybox to /bin/busybox.nosuid. \
						busybox rm -f $link \
						busybox ln -s $to $link \
					fi \
				done < /etc/busybox.links$suffix \
			fi \
		done \
	fi \
"

# $DESCRIPTION_busybox-dev
#   rename from DESCRIPTION_${PN}-dev data.py:170 [expandKeys]
#     "${DESCRIPTION}  This package contains symbolic links, header files, and related items necessary for software development."
DESCRIPTION_busybox-dev="BusyBox combines tiny versions of many common UNIX utilities into a single small executable. It provides minimalist replacements for most of the utilities you usually find in GNU fileutils, shellutils, etc. The utilities in BusyBox generally have fewer options than their full-featured GNU cousins; however, the options that are included provide the expected functionality and behave very much like their GNU counterparts. BusyBox provides a fairly complete POSIX environment for any small or embedded system.  This package contains symbolic links, header files, and related items necessary for software development."

# $DESCRIPTION_busybox-dbg
#   rename from DESCRIPTION_${PN}-dbg data.py:170 [expandKeys]
#     "${DESCRIPTION}  This package contains ELF symbols and related sources for debugging purposes."
DESCRIPTION_busybox-dbg="BusyBox combines tiny versions of many common UNIX utilities into a single small executable. It provides minimalist replacements for most of the utilities you usually find in GNU fileutils, shellutils, etc. The utilities in BusyBox generally have fewer options than their full-featured GNU cousins; however, the options that are included provide the expected functionality and behave very much like their GNU counterparts. BusyBox provides a fairly complete POSIX environment for any small or embedded system.  This package contains ELF symbols and related sources for debugging purposes."

#     "${DESCRIPTION}  This package contains static libraries for software development."
DESCRIPTION_busybox-staticdev="BusyBox combines tiny versions of many common UNIX utilities into a single small executable. It provides minimalist replacements for most of the utilities you usually find in GNU fileutils, shellutils, etc. The utilities in BusyBox generally have fewer options than their full-featured GNU cousins; however, the options that are included provide the expected functionality and behave very much like their GNU counterparts. BusyBox provides a fairly complete POSIX environment for any small or embedded system.  This package contains static libraries for software development."

DESCRIPTION_busybox-ptest="BusyBox combines tiny versions of many common UNIX utilities into a single small executable. It provides minimalist replacements for most of the utilities you usually find in GNU fileutils, shellutils, etc. The utilities in BusyBox generally have fewer options than their full-featured GNU cousins; however, the options that are included provide the expected functionality and behave very much like their GNU counterparts. BusyBox provides a fairly complete POSIX environment for any small or embedded system.  This package contains a test directory /usr/lib/busybox/ptest for package test purposes."

#
# $pkg_prerm_busybox
#   rename from pkg_prerm_${PN} data.py:170 [expandKeys]
#     "	# This is so you can make busybox commit suicide - removing busybox with no other packages
#     	# providing its files, this will make update-alternatives work, but the update-rc.d part
#     	# for syslog, httpd and/or udhcpd will fail if there is no other package providing sh
#     	tmpdir=`mktemp -d /tmp/busyboxrm-XXXXXX`
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/[
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/test
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/head
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sh
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/basename
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/echo
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/mv
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/ln
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/dirname
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/rm
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sed
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sort
#     	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/grep
#     	export PATH=$PATH:$tmpdir
#     "
pkg_prerm_busybox="	# This is so you can make busybox commit suicide - removing busybox with no other packages \
	# providing its files, this will make update-alternatives work, but the update-rc.d part \
	# for syslog, httpd and/or udhcpd will fail if there is no other package providing sh \
	tmpdir=`mktemp -d /tmp/busyboxrm-XXXXXX` \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/[ \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/test \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/head \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sh \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/basename \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/echo \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/mv \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/ln \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/dirname \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/rm \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sed \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/sort \
	ln -s /bin/busybox $tmpdir/grep \
	export PATH=$PATH:$tmpdir \
"
#

process_file="def process_file_linux(cmd, fpath, basedir, tmpdir, d): \
    import subprocess as sub \
 \
    p = sub.Popen([cmd, '-l', fpath],stdout=sub.PIPE,stderr=sub.PIPE) \
    err, out = p.communicate() \
    # If returned succesfully, process stderr for results \
    if p.returncode != 0: \
        return \
 \
    # Throw away everything other than the rpath list \
    curr_rpath = err.partition(\"RPATH=\")[2] \
    #bb.note(\"Current rpath for %s is %s\" % (fpath, curr_rpath.strip())) \
    rpaths = curr_rpath.split(\":\") \
    new_rpaths = [] \
    for rpath in rpaths: \
        # If rpath is already dynamic copy it to new_rpath and continue \
        if rpath.find(\"$ORIGIN\") != -1: \
            new_rpaths.append(rpath.strip()) \
            continue \
        rpath =  os.path.normpath(rpath) \
        # If the rpath shares a root with base_prefix determine a new dynamic rpath from the \
        # base_prefix shared root \
        if rpath.find(basedir) != -1: \
            depth = fpath.partition(basedir)[2].count('/') \
            libpath = rpath.partition(basedir)[2].strip() \
        # otherwise (i.e. cross packages) determine a shared root based on the TMPDIR \
        # NOTE: This will not work reliably for cross packages, particularly in the case \
        # where your TMPDIR is a short path (i.e. /usr/poky) as chrpath cannot insert an \
        # rpath longer than that which is already set. \
        elif rpath.find(tmpdir) != -1: \
            depth = fpath.rpartition(tmpdir)[2].count('/') \
            libpath = rpath.partition(tmpdir)[2].strip() \
        else: \
            new_rpaths.append(rpath.strip()) \
            return \
        base = \"$ORIGIN\" \
        while depth > 1: \
            base += \"/..\" \
            depth-=1 \
        new_rpaths.append(\"%s%s\" % (base, libpath)) \
 \
    # if we have modified some rpaths call chrpath to update the binary \
    if len(new_rpaths): \
        args = \":\".join(new_rpaths) \
        #bb.note(\"Setting rpath for %s to %s\" %(fpath, args)) \
        p = sub.Popen([cmd, '-r', args, fpath],stdout=sub.PIPE,stderr=sub.PIPE) \
        out, err = p.communicate() \
        if p.returncode != 0: \
            bb.error(\"%s: chrpath command failed with exit code %d:\n%s%s\" % (d.getVar('PN', True), p.returncode, out, err)) \
            raise bb.build.FuncFailed \
"
#

systemd_postinst() {
OPTS=""

if [ -n "$D" ]; then
    OPTS="--root=$D"
fi

if type systemctl >/dev/null 2>/dev/null; then
	systemctl $OPTS enable ${SYSTEMD_SERVICE}

	if [ -z "$D" -a "enable" = "enable" ]; then
		systemctl restart ${SYSTEMD_SERVICE}
	fi
fi

}

do_install_ptest_base() {
    if [ 0 = 1 ]; then
        if [ -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/run-ptest ]; then
            install -D /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/run-ptest /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/lib/busybox/ptest/run-ptest
            if grep -q install-ptest: Makefile; then
                oe_runmake DESTDIR=/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/lib/busybox/ptest install-ptest
            fi
            do_install_ptest
        fi
    fi

}

updatercd_postinst() {
if test "x$D" != "x"; then
	OPT="-r $D"
else
	OPT="-s"
fi
if type update-rc.d >/dev/null 2>/dev/null; then
	update-rc.d $OPT ${INITSCRIPT_NAME} defaults
fi

}

prelink_image() {
#	export PSEUDO_DEBUG=4
#	/bin/env | /bin/grep PSEUDO
#	echo "LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$LD_LIBRARY_PATH"
#	echo "LD_PRELOAD=$LD_PRELOAD"

	pre_prelink_size=`du -ks /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs | awk '{size = $1 ; print size }'`
	echo "Size before prelinking $pre_prelink_size."

	# We need a prelink conf on the filesystem, add one if it's missing
	if [ ! -e /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/etc/prelink.conf ]; then
		cp /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/x86_64-linux/etc/prelink.conf \
			/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/etc/prelink.conf
		dummy_prelink_conf=true;
	else
		dummy_prelink_conf=false;
	fi

	# prelink!
	/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/x86_64-linux/usr/sbin/prelink --root /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs -amR -N -c /etc/prelink.conf

	# Remove the prelink.conf if we had to add it.
	if [ "$dummy_prelink_conf" = "true" ]; then
		rm -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/etc/prelink.conf
	fi

	pre_prelink_size=`du -ks /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs | awk '{size = $1 ; print size }'`
	echo "Size after prelinking $pre_prelink_size."

}

bbdebug() {
	USAGE='Usage: bbdebug [123] "message"'
	if [ $# -lt 2 ]; then
		bbfatal "$USAGE"
	fi

	# Strip off the debug level and ensure it is an integer
	DBGLVL=$1; shift
	if ! [[ "$DBGLVL" =~ ^[0-9]+ ]]; then
		bbfatal "$USAGE"
	fi

	# All debug output is printed to the logs
	echo "DEBUG: $*"

}

bbnote() {
	echo "NOTE: $*"

}

systemd_prerm() {
if type systemctl >/dev/null 2>/dev/null; then
	if [ -z "$D" ]; then
		systemctl stop ${SYSTEMD_SERVICE}
	fi

	systemctl disable ${SYSTEMD_SERVICE}
fi

}

oe_machinstall() {
	# Purpose: Install machine dependent files, if available
	#          If not available, check if there is a default
	#          If no default, just touch the destination
	# Example:
	#                $1  $2   $3         $4
	# oe_machinstall -m 0644 fstab /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/fstab
	#
	# TODO: Check argument number?
	#
	filename=`basename $3`
	dirname=`dirname $3`

	for o in `echo linux:i586:build-linux:pn-busybox:x86:eurotech-isis:duma:class-target:forcevariable:libc-glibc | tr ':' ' '`; do
		if [ -e $dirname/$o/$filename ]; then
			bbnote $dirname/$o/$filename present, installing to $4
			install $1 $2 $dirname/$o/$filename $4
			return
		fi
	done
#	bbnote overrides specific file NOT present, trying default=$3...
	if [ -e $3 ]; then
		bbnote $3 present, installing to $4
		install $1 $2 $3 $4
	else
		bbnote $3 NOT present, touching empty $4
		touch $4
	fi

}

	cml1_do_configure

}

	oe_runmake oldconfig

}

do_prepare_config() {
	sed -e 's#@DATADIR@#/usr/share#g' \
		< /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/defconfig > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config
	sed -i -e '/CONFIG_STATIC/d' .config
	echo "# CONFIG_STATIC is not set" >> .config
	for i in 'CROSS' 'DISTRO FEATURES'; do echo "### $i"; done >> \
		/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config
	sed -i -e '/CROSS_COMPILER_PREFIX/d; 		/CONFIG_EXTRA_CFLAGS/d; 		/^[# ]*CONFIG_FEATURE_IPV6[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_LFS[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_FDISK_SUPPORT_LARGE_DISKS[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_LOCALE_SUPPORT[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_FEATURE_IFUPDOWN_IPV4[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_FEATURE_IFUPDOWN_IPV6[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_RFKILL[ =]/d
/^[# ]*CONFIG_RFKILL[ =]/d
/^### DISTRO FEATURES$/a\
CONFIG_FEATURE_IPV6=y\nCONFIG_LFS=y\nCONFIG_FDISK_SUPPORT_LARGE_DISKS=y\n# CONFIG_LOCALE_SUPPORT is not set\nCONFIG_FEATURE_IFUPDOWN_IPV4=y\nCONFIG_FEATURE_IFUPDOWN_IPV6=y\n# CONFIG_RFKILL is not set\n# CONFIG_RFKILL is not set

/^### CROSS$/a\
CONFIG_CROSS_COMPILER_PREFIX="i586-poky-linux-"\nCONFIG_EXTRA_CFLAGS=" -O2 -pipe -g -feliminate-unused-debug-types" " -m32 -march=core2 -msse3 -mtune=generic -mfpmath=sse"
' /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config
	if test 1 -eq 0 && test 1 -eq 0; then
	  # disable networking applets
	  mv /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config.oe-tmp
	  awk 'BEGIN{net=0}
	  /^# Networking Utilities/{net=1}
	  /^#$/{if(net){net=net+1}}
	  {if(net==2&&$0 !~ /^#/&&$1){print("# "$1" is not set")}else{print}}' \
		  /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config.oe-tmp > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config
	fi

}

	OPT=""
fi
if type update-rc.d >/dev/null 2>/dev/null; then
	update-rc.d $OPT ${INITSCRIPT_NAME} remove
fi

}

create_wrapper() {
	# Create a wrapper script where extra environment variables are needed
	#
	# These are useful to work around relocation issues, by setting environment
	# variables which point to paths in the filesystem.
	#
	# Usage: create_wrapper FILENAME [[VAR=VALUE]..]

	cmd=$1
	shift

	echo "Generating wrapper script for $cmd"

	mv $cmd $cmd.real
	cmdname=`basename $cmd`
	cat <<END >$cmd
#!/bin/bash
realpath=\`readlink -fn \$0\`
export $@
exec -a \`dirname \$realpath\`/$cmdname \`dirname \$realpath\`/$cmdname.real "\$@"
END
	chmod +x $cmd

}

bbplain() {
	echo "$*"

}

sstate_create_package() {
	cd ${SSTATE_BUILDDIR}
	TFILE=`mktemp /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/sstate-cache/IN/sstate-busybox-core2-poky-linux-1.21.1-r0-core2-3-INVALID.XXXXXXXX`
	# Need to handle empty directories
	if [ "$(ls -A)" ]; then
		set +e
		tar -czf $TFILE *
		if [ $? -ne 0 ] && [ $? -ne 1 ]; then
			exit 1
		fi
		set -e
	else
		tar -cz --file=$TFILE --files-from=/dev/null
	fi
	chmod 0664 $TFILE
	mv -f $TFILE /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/sstate-cache/IN/sstate-busybox-core2-poky-linux-1.21.1-r0-core2-3-INVALID

	cd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0
	rm -rf ${SSTATE_BUILDDIR}

}

ldconfig_postinst_fragment() {
if [ x"$D" = "x" ]; then
	if [ -x /sbin/ldconfig ]; then /sbin/ldconfig ; fi
fi

}

deb_log_check() {
	target="$1"
	lf_path="$2"

	lf_txt="`cat $lf_path`"
	for keyword_die in "^E:"
	do
		if (echo "$lf_txt" | grep -v log_check | grep "$keyword_die") >/dev/null 2>&1
		then
			echo "log_check: There were error messages in the logfile"
			printf "log_check: Matched keyword: [$keyword_die]\n\n"
			echo "$lf_txt" | grep -v log_check | grep -C 5 -i "$keyword_die"
			echo ""
			do_exit=1
		fi
	done
	test "$do_exit" = 1 && exit 1
	true

}

sysroot_stage_libdir() {
	src="$1"
	dest="$2"

	sysroot_stage_dir $src $dest

}

	:

}

die() {
	bbfatal "$*"

}

	:

}

do_compile() {
	unset CFLAGS CPPFLAGS CXXFLAGS LDFLAGS
	if [ "1" = "1" -a x`grep "CONFIG_FEATURE_INDIVIDUAL=y" .config` = x ]; then
	# split the .config into two parts, and make two busybox binaries
		cp .config .config.orig
		oe_runmake busybox.cfg.suid
		oe_runmake busybox.cfg.nosuid
		for i in `cat busybox.cfg.suid busybox.cfg.nosuid`; do
			echo "# $i is not set" >> .config.disable.apps
		done
		merge_config.sh -m .config.orig .config.disable.apps
		cp .config .config.nonapps
		for s in suid nosuid; do
			cat busybox.cfg.$s | while read item; do
				grep -w "$item" .config.orig
			done > .config.app.$s
			merge_config.sh -m .config.nonapps .config.app.$s
			oe_runmake busybox_unstripped
			mv busybox_unstripped busybox.$s
			oe_runmake busybox.links
			mv busybox.links busybox.links.$s
		done
		# copy .config.orig back to .config, because the install process may check this file
		cp .config.orig .config
		# cleanup
		rm .config.orig .config.app.suid .config.app.nosuid .config.disable.apps .config.nonapps
	else
		oe_runmake busybox_unstripped
		cp busybox_unstripped busybox
		oe_runmake busybox.links
	fi

}

base_do_package() {
	:

}

oe_soinstall() {
	# Purpose: Install shared library file and
	#          create the necessary links
	# Example:
	#
	# oe_
	#
	#bbnote installing shared library $1 to $2
	#
	libname=`basename $1`
	install -m 755 $1 $2/$libname
	sonamelink=`i586-poky-linux-readelf -d $1 |grep 'Library soname:' |sed -e 's/.*\[\(.*\)\].*/\1/'`
	solink=`echo $libname | sed -e 's/\.so\..*/.so/'`
	ln -sf $libname $2/$sonamelink
	ln -sf $libname $2/$solink

}

    fi

        cp /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config      /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/lib/busybox/ptest/

create_cmdline_wrapper() {
	# Create a wrapper script where commandline options are needed
	#
	# These are useful to work around relocation issues, by passing extra options
	# to a program
	#
	# Usage: create_cmdline_wrapper FILENAME <extra-options>

	cmd=$1
	shift

	echo "Generating wrapper script for $cmd"

	mv $cmd $cmd.real
	cmdname=`basename $cmd`.real
	cat <<END >$cmd
#!/bin/bash
realpath=\`readlink -fn \$0\`
exec -a $cmd \`dirname \$realpath\`/$cmdname $@ "\$@"
END
	chmod +x $cmd

}

oe_libinstall() {
	# Purpose: Install a library, in all its forms
	# Example
	#
	# oe_libinstall libltdl /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/eurotech-isis/usr/lib/
	# oe_libinstall -C src/libblah libblah /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image//usr/lib/
	dir=""
	libtool=""
	silent=""
	require_static=""
	require_shared=""
	staging_install=""
	while [ "$#" -gt 0 ]; do
		case "$1" in
		-C)
			shift
			dir="$1"
			;;
		-s)
			silent=1
			;;
		-a)
			require_static=1
			;;
		-so)
			require_shared=1
			;;
		-*)
			bbfatal "oe_libinstall: unknown option: $1"
			;;
		*)
			break;
			;;
		esac
		shift
	done

	libname="$1"
	shift
	destpath="$1"
	if [ -z "$destpath" ]; then
		bbfatal "oe_libinstall: no destination path specified"
	fi
	if echo "$destpath/" | egrep '^/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/eurotech-isis/usr/lib/' >/dev/null
	then
		staging_install=1
	fi

	__runcmd () {
		if [ -z "$silent" ]; then
			echo >&2 "oe_libinstall: $*"
		fi
		$*
	}

	if [ -z "$dir" ]; then
		dir=`pwd`
	fi

	dotlai=$libname.lai

	# Sanity check that the libname.lai is unique
	number_of_files=`(cd $dir; find . -name "$dotlai") | wc -l`
	if [ $number_of_files -gt 1 ]; then
		bbfatal "oe_libinstall: $dotlai is not unique in $dir"
	fi


	dir=$dir`(cd $dir;find . -name "$dotlai") | sed "s/^\.//;s/\/$dotlai\$//;q"`
	olddir=`pwd`
	__runcmd cd $dir

	lafile=$libname.la

	# If such file doesn't exist, try to cut version suffix
	if [ ! -f "$lafile" ]; then
		libname1=`echo "$libname" | sed 's/-[0-9.]*$//'`
		lafile1=$libname.la
		if [ -f "$lafile1" ]; then
			libname=$libname1
			lafile=$lafile1
		fi
	fi

	if [ -f "$lafile" ]; then
		# libtool archive
		eval `cat $lafile|grep "^library_names="`
		libtool=1
	else
		library_names="$libname.so* $libname.dll.a $libname.*.dylib"
	fi

	__runcmd install -d $destpath/
	dota=$libname.a
	if [ -f "$dota" -o -n "$require_static" ]; then
		rm -f $destpath/$dota
		__runcmd install -m 0644 $dota $destpath/
	fi
	if [ -f "$dotlai" -a -n "$libtool" ]; then
		rm -f $destpath/$libname.la
		__runcmd install -m 0644 $dotlai $destpath/$libname.la
	fi

	for name in $library_names; do
		files=`eval echo $name`
		for f in $files; do
			if [ ! -e "$f" ]; then
				if [ -n "$libtool" ]; then
					bbfatal "oe_libinstall: $dir/$f not found."
				fi
			elif [ -L "$f" ]; then
				__runcmd cp -P "$f" $destpath/
			elif [ ! -L "$f" ]; then
				libfile="$f"
				rm -f $destpath/$libfile
				__runcmd install -m 0755 $libfile $destpath/
			fi
		done
	done

	if [ -z "$libfile" ]; then
		if  [ -n "$require_shared" ]; then
			bbfatal "oe_libinstall: unable to locate shared library"
		fi
	elif [ -z "$libtool" ]; then
		# special case hack for non-libtool .so.#.#.# links
		baselibfile=`basename "$libfile"`
		if (echo $baselibfile | grep -qE '^lib.*\.so\.[0-9.]*$'); then
			sonamelink=`i586-poky-linux-readelf -d $libfile |grep 'Library soname:' |sed -e 's/.*\[\(.*\)\].*/\1/'`
			solink=`echo $baselibfile | sed -e 's/\.so\..*/.so/'`
			if [ -n "$sonamelink" -a x"$baselibfile" != x"$sonamelink" ]; then
				__runcmd ln -sf $baselibfile $destpath/$sonamelink
			fi
			__runcmd ln -sf $baselibfile $destpath/$solink
		fi
	fi

	__runcmd cd "$olddir"

}

base_do_compile() {
	if [ -e Makefile -o -e makefile -o -e GNUmakefile ]; then
		oe_runmake || die "make failed"
	else
		bbnote "nothing to compile"
	fi

}

bbfatal() {
	echo "ERROR: $*"
	exit 1

}

package_update_index_deb() {

	local debarchs=""

	if [ ! -z "${DEPLOY_KEEP_PACKAGES}" ]; then
		return
	fi

	for arch in all any noarch x86 i386 i486 i586 i686 core2 eurotech_isis all any noarch x86_64-nativesdk; do
		if [ -e /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb/$arch ]; then
			debarchs="$debarchs $arch"
		fi
	done

	found=0
	for arch in $debarchs; do
		if [ ! -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb/$arch ]; then
			continue;
		fi
		cd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb/$arch
		dpkg-scanpackages . | gzip > Packages.gz
		echo "Label: $arch" > Release
		found=1
	done
	if [ "$found" != "1" ]; then
		bbfatal "There are no packages in /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb!"
	fi

}

sysroot_stage_dir() {
	src="$1"
	dest="$2"
	# if the src doesn't exist don't do anything
	if [ ! -d "$src" ]; then
		 return
	fi

	# We only want to stage the contents of $src if it's non-empty so first rmdir $src
	# then if it still exists (rmdir on non-empty dir fails) we can copy its contents
	rmdir "$src" 2> /dev/null || true
	# However we always want to stage a $src itself, even if it's empty
	mkdir -p "$dest"
	if [ -d "$src" ]; then
		tar -cf - -C "$src" -p . | tar -xf - -C "$dest"
	fi

}

bberror() {
	echo "ERROR: $*"

}

bbwarn() {
	echo "WARNING: $*"

}

do_install() {
	if [ "/usr" != "/usr" ]; then
		sed -i "s:^/usr/:/usr/:" busybox.links*
	fi
	if [ "/sbin" != "/sbin" ]; then
		sed -i "s:^/sbin/:/sbin/:" busybox.links*
	fi

	install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d

	if ! grep -q "CONFIG_FEATURE_INDIVIDUAL=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		# Install /bin/busybox, and the /bin/sh link so the postinst script
		# can run. Let update-alternatives handle the rest.
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin
		if [ "1" = "1" ]; then
			install -m 4755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.suid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin
			install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.nosuid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin
			install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.links.suid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc
			install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.links.nosuid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc
			ln -sf busybox.nosuid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/sh
			# Keep a default busybox for people who want to invoke busybox directly.
			# This is also useful for the on device upgrade. Because we want
			# to use the busybox command in postinst.
			ln -sf busybox.nosuid /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/busybox
		else
			if grep -q "CONFIG_FEATURE_SUID=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
				install -m 4755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin
			else
				install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin
			fi
			install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.links /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc
			ln -sf busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/sh
			# We make this symlink here to eliminate the error when upgrading together
			# with busybox-syslog. Without this symlink, the opkg may think of the
			# busybox.nosuid as obsolete and remove it, resulting in dead links like
			# /bin/sed -> /bin/busybox.nosuid. This will make upgrading busybox-syslog fail.
			# This symlink will be safely deleted in postinst, thus no negative effect.
			ln -sf busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/busybox.nosuid
		fi
	else
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/sbin
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/lib /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/bin /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/sbin
		cat busybox.links | while read FILE; do
			NAME=`basename "$FILE"`
			install -m 0755 "0_lib/$NAME" "/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image$FILE.busybox"
		done
		# add suid bit where needed
		for i in `grep -E "APPLET.*BB_SUID_((MAYBE|REQUIRE))" include/applets.h | grep -v _BB_SUID_DROP | cut -f 3 -d '(' | cut -f 1 -d ','`; do
			find /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image -name $i.busybox -exec chmod a+s {} \;
		done
		install -m 0755 0_lib/libbusybox.so.1.21.1 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/lib/libbusybox.so.1.21.1
		ln -sf sh.busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/sh
		ln -sf ln.busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/bin/ln
		ln -sf test.busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/bin/test
		if [ -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/linuxrc.busybox ]; then
			mv /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/linuxrc.busybox /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/linuxrc
		fi
		install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/busybox.links /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc
	fi

	if grep -q "CONFIG_SYSLOGD=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/syslog /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/syslog.busybox
		install -m 644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/syslog-startup.conf /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/syslog-startup.conf.busybox
		install -m 644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/syslog.conf /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/syslog.conf.busybox
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_CROND=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-cron /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_HTTPD=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-httpd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/srv/www
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_UDHCPD=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-udhcpd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_HWCLOCK=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/hwclock.sh /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_UDHCPC=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/udhcpc.d
		install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/share/udhcpc
                install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/simple.script /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/udhcpc.d/50default
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/default.script /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/usr/share/udhcpc/default.script
	fi
	if grep "CONFIG_INETD=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
		install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/inetd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/inetd.busybox
		sed -i "s:/usr/sbin/:/usr/sbin/:" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/inetd.busybox
		install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/inetd.conf /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/
	fi
        if grep "CONFIG_MDEV=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
               install -m 0755 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mdev /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/init.d/mdev
               if grep "CONFIG_FEATURE_MDEV_CONF=y" /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-1.21.1/.config; then
                       install -m 644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mdev.conf /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/mdev.conf
               fi
	fi

    if true; then
        install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/lib/systemd/system
        sed 's,@base_sbindir@,/sbin,g' < /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-syslog.service.in \
            > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/lib/systemd/system/busybox-syslog.service
        sed 's,@base_sbindir@,/sbin,g' < /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-klogd.service.in \
            > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/lib/systemd/system/busybox-klogd.service

        if [ -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-syslog.default ] ; then
            install -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/default
            install -m 0644 /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/busybox-syslog.default /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/default/busybox-syslog
        fi

        ln -sf /dev/null /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/lib/systemd/system/syslog.service
    fi

    # Remove the sysvinit specific configuration file for systemd systems to avoid confusion
    if true; then
	rm -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/image/etc/syslog-startup.conf.busybox
    fi

}

sysroot_stage_dirs() {
	from="$1"
	to="$2"

	sysroot_stage_dir $from/usr/include $to/usr/include
	if [ "x86_64-linux" = "i586-poky-linux" ]; then
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/usr/bin $to/usr/bin
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/usr/sbin $to/usr/sbin
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/bin $to/bin
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/sbin $to/sbin
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/usr/lib/busybox $to/usr/lib/busybox
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/etc $to/etc
		sysroot_stage_dir $from/var $to/var
	fi
	if [ -d $from/usr/lib ]
	then
		sysroot_stage_libdir $from//usr/lib $to/usr/lib
	fi
	if [ -d $from/lib ]
	then
		sysroot_stage_libdir $from/lib $to/lib
	fi
	if [ -d $from/lib ]
	then
		sysroot_stage_libdir $from/lib $to/lib
	fi
	sysroot_stage_dir $from/usr/share $to/usr/share
	# We don't care about docs/info/manpages/locales
	rm -rf $to/usr/share/man/ $to/usr/share/doc/ $to/usr/share/info/ ${to}/usr/share/locale/
	rm -rf $to/usr/share/applications/ $to/usr/share/fonts/ $to/usr/share/pixmaps/

}

package_install_internal_deb() {

	local target_rootfs="${INSTALL_ROOTFS_DEB}"
	local dpkg_arch="${INSTALL_BASEARCH_DEB}"
	local archs="${INSTALL_ARCHS_DEB}"
	local package_to_install="${INSTALL_PACKAGES_NORMAL_DEB}"
	local package_attemptonly="${INSTALL_PACKAGES_ATTEMPTONLY_DEB}"
	local package_linguas="${INSTALL_PACKAGES_LINGUAS_DEB}"
	local task="${INSTALL_TASK_DEB}"

	mkdir -p /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt
	rm -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/sources.list.rev
	rm -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/preferences

	priority=1
	for arch in $archs; do
		if [ ! -d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb/$arch ]; then
			continue;
		fi

		echo "deb file:/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/deb/$arch/ ./" >> /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/sources.list.rev
		(echo "Package: *"
		echo "Pin: release l=$arch"
		echo "Pin-Priority: $(expr 800 + $priority)"
		echo) >> /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/preferences
		priority=$(expr $priority + 5)
	done

	for pkg in ${PACKAGE_EXCLUDE}; do
		(echo "Package: $pkg"
		echo "Pin: release *"
		echo "Pin-Priority: -1"
		echo) >> /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/preferences
	done

	tac /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/sources.list.rev > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/sources.list

	# The params in deb package control don't allow character `_', so
	# change the arch's `_' to `-' in it.
	dpkg_arch=`echo ${dpkg_arch} | sed 's/_/-/g'`
	cat "/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/x86_64-linux/etc/apt/apt.conf.sample" \
		| sed -e "s#Architecture \".*\";#Architecture \"${dpkg_arch}\";#" \
		| sed -e "s:#ROOTFS#:${target_rootfs}:g" \
		| sed -e "s:#APTCONF#:/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt:g" \
		> "/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/apt.conf"

	export APT_CONFIG="/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/apt/apt.conf"

	mkdir -p ${target_rootfs}/var/lib/dpkg/info
	mkdir -p ${target_rootfs}/var/lib/dpkg/updates

	> ${target_rootfs}/var/lib/dpkg/status
	> ${target_rootfs}/var/lib/dpkg/available

	apt-get update

	if [ ! -z "${package_linguas}" ]; then
		for i in ${package_linguas}; do
			apt-get  install $i --force-yes --allow-unauthenticated
			if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
				exit 1
			fi
		done
	fi

	# normal install
	if [ ! -z "${package_to_install}" ]; then
		apt-get  install ${package_to_install} --force-yes --allow-unauthenticated
		if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
			exit 1
		fi

		# Attempt to correct the probable broken dependencies in place.
		apt-get  -f install
		if [ $? -ne 0 ]; then
			exit 1
		fi
	fi

	rm -f `dirname ${BB_LOGFILE}`/log.do_${task}-attemptonly.${PID}
	if [ ! -z "${package_attemptonly}" ]; then
		for i in ${package_attemptonly}; do
			apt-get  install $i --force-yes --allow-unauthenticated >> `dirname ${BB_LOGFILE}`/log.do_${task}-attemptonly.${PID} 2>&1 || true
		done
	fi

	find ${target_rootfs} -name \*.dpkg-new | for i in `cat`; do
		mv $i `echo $i | sed -e's,\.dpkg-new$,,'`
	done

	# Mark all packages installed
	sed -i -e "s/Status: install ok unpacked/Status: install ok installed/;" ${target_rootfs}/var/lib/dpkg/status

}

license_create_manifest() {
	mkdir -p /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/busybox-eurotech-isis-20140514080235
	# Get list of installed packages
	list_installed_packages |sort > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/busybox-eurotech-isis-20140514080235/package.manifest
	INSTALLED_PKGS=`cat /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/busybox-eurotech-isis-20140514080235/package.manifest`
	LICENSE_MANIFEST="/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/busybox-eurotech-isis-20140514080235/license.manifest"
	# remove existing license.manifest file
	if [ -f ${LICENSE_MANIFEST} ]; then
		rm ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
	fi
	touch ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
	for pkg in ${INSTALLED_PKGS}; do
		filename=`ls /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/eurotech-isis/pkgdata/runtime-reverse/${pkg}| head -1`
		pkged_pn="$(sed -n 's/^PN: //p' ${filename})"

		# check to see if the package name exists in the manifest. if so, bail.
		if grep -q "^PACKAGE NAME: ${pkg}" ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}; then
			continue
		fi

		pkged_pv="$(sed -n 's/^PV: //p' ${filename})"
		pkged_name="$(basename $(readlink ${filename}))"
		pkged_lic="$(sed -n "/^LICENSE_${pkged_name}: /{ s/^LICENSE_${pkged_name}: //; s/[|&()*]/ /g; s/  */ /g; p }" ${filename})"
		if [ -z ${pkged_lic} ]; then
			# fallback checking value of LICENSE
			pkged_lic="$(sed -n "/^LICENSE: /{ s/^LICENSE: //; s/[|&()*]/ /g; s/  */ /g; p }" ${filename})"
		fi

		echo "PACKAGE NAME:" ${pkg} >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
		echo "PACKAGE VERSION:" ${pkged_pv} >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
		echo "RECIPE NAME:" ${pkged_pn} >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
		printf "LICENSE:" >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
		for lic in ${pkged_lic}; do
			# to reference a license file trim trailing + symbol
			if ! [ -e "/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/${pkged_pn}/generic_${lic%+}" ]; then
				bbwarn "The license listed ${lic} was not in the licenses collected for ${pkged_pn}"
			fi
                        printf " ${lic}" >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
		done
		printf "\n\n" >> ${LICENSE_MANIFEST}
	done

	# Two options here:
	# - Just copy the manifest
	# - Copy the manifest and the license directories
	# With both options set we see a .5 M increase in core-image-minimal
	if [ -n "${COPY_LIC_MANIFEST}" ]; then
		mkdir -p /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/
		cp ${LICENSE_MANIFEST} /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/license.manifest
		if [ -n "${COPY_LIC_DIRS}" ]; then
			for pkg in ${INSTALLED_PKGS}; do
				mkdir -p /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/${pkg}
				for lic in `ls /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/${pkg}`; do
					# Really don't need to copy the generics as they're
					# represented in the manifest and in the actual pkg licenses
					# Doing so would make your image quite a bit larger
					if [ "${lic#generic_}" = "${lic}" ]; then
						cp /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/${pkg}/${lic} /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/${pkg}/${lic}
					else
						if [ ! -f /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/${lic} ]; then
							cp /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/deploy/licenses/${pkg}/${lic} /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/
						fi
						ln -s ../${lic} /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs/usr/share/common-licenses/${pkg}/${lic}
					fi
				done
			done
		fi
	fi


}

mklibs_optimize_image() {
	for img in ${MKLIBS_OPTIMIZED_IMAGES}
	do
		if [ "${img}" = "busybox" ] || [ "${img}" = "all" ]
		then
			mklibs_optimize_image_doit
			break
		fi
	done

}

	bbnote make -e MAKEFLAGS= V=1 ARCH=i586 CROSS_COMPILE=i586-poky-linux- SKIP_STRIP=y "$@"
	make -e MAKEFLAGS= V=1 ARCH=i586 CROSS_COMPILE=i586-poky-linux- SKIP_STRIP=y "$@" || die "oe_runmake failed"

}

mklibs_optimize_image_doit() {
	rm -rf /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs
	mkdir -p /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/dest
	cd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs
	du -bs > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/du.before.mklibs.txt
	for i in `find .`; do file $i; done \
		| grep ELF \
		| grep "LSB *executable" \
		| grep "dynamically linked" \
		| sed "s/:.*//" \
		| sed "s+^\./++" \
		> /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/executables.list

	case i586 in
		powerpc | mips | microblaze )
			dynamic_loader="/lib/ld.so.1"
			;;
		powerpc64)
			dynamic_loader="/lib/ld64.so.1"
			;;
		x86_64)
			dynamic_loader="/lib/ld-linux-x86-64.so.2"
			;;
		i586 )
			dynamic_loader="/lib/ld-linux.so.2"
			;;
		arm )
			dynamic_loader="/lib/ld-linux.so.3"
			;;
		* )
			dynamic_loader="/unknown_dynamic_linker"
			;;
	esac

	mklibs -v \
		--ldlib ${dynamic_loader} \
		--libdir lib \
		--sysroot /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/eurotech-isis \
		--gcc-options "--sysroot=/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sysroots/eurotech-isis" \
		--root /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs \
		--target `echo i586-poky-linux- | sed 's/-$//' ` \
		-d /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/dest \
		`cat /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/executables.list`

	cd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/dest
	for i in *
	do
		cp $i `find /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs -name $i`
	done

	cd /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/rootfs
	du -bs > /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/du.after.mklibs.txt

	echo rootfs size before mklibs optimization: `cat /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/du.before.mklibs.txt`
	echo rootfs size after mklibs optimization: `cat /home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/work/core2-poky-linux/busybox/1.21.1-r0/mklibs/du.after.mklibs.txt`

}



python check_connectivity () {
def check_connectivity(d):
    # URI's to check can be set in the CONNECTIVITY_CHECK_URIS variable
    # using the same syntax as for SRC_URI. If the variable is not set
    # the check is skipped
    test_uris = (d.getVar('CONNECTIVITY_CHECK_URIS', True) or "").split()
    retval = ""

    # Only check connectivity if network enabled and the
    # CONNECTIVITY_CHECK_URIS are set
    network_enabled = not d.getVar('BB_NO_NETWORK', True)
    check_enabled = len(test_uris)
    # Take a copy of the data store and unset MIRRORS and PREMIRROS
    data = bb.data.createCopy(d)
    data.delVar('PREMIRRORS')
    data.delVar('MIRRORS')
    if check_enabled and network_enabled:
        try:
            fetcher = bb.fetch2.Fetch(test_uris, data)
            fetcher.checkstatus()
        except Exception:
            # Allow the message to be configured so that users can be
            # pointed to a support mechanism.
            msg = data.getVar('CONNECTIVITY_CHECK_MSG', True) or ""
            if len(msg) == 0:
                msg = "Failed to fetch test data from the network. Please ensure your network is configured correctly.\n"
            retval = msg

    return retval
}


python sstate_install () {
def sstate_install(ss, d):
    import oe.path
    import subprocess

    sharedfiles = []
    shareddirs = []
    bb.utils.mkdirhier(d.expand("/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sstate-control"))

    d2 = d.createCopy()
    extrainf = d.getVarFlag("do_" + ss['task'], 'stamp-extra-info', True)
    if extrainf:
        d2.setVar("SSTATE_MANMACH", extrainf)
    manifest = d2.expand("/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sstate-control/manifest-core2-busybox.%s" % ss['name'])

    if os.access(manifest, os.R_OK):
        bb.fatal("Package already staged (%s)?!" % manifest)

    locks = []
    for lock in ss['lockfiles-shared']:
        locks.append(bb.utils.lockfile(lock, True))
    for lock in ss['lockfiles']:
        locks.append(bb.utils.lockfile(lock))

    for state in ss['dirs']:
        bb.debug(2, "Staging files from %s to %s" % (state[1], state[2]))
        for walkroot, dirs, files in os.walk(state[1]):
            for file in files:
                srcpath = os.path.join(walkroot, file)
                dstpath = srcpath.replace(state[1], state[2])
                #bb.debug(2, "Staging %s to %s" % (srcpath, dstpath))
                sharedfiles.append(dstpath)
            for dir in dirs:
                srcdir = os.path.join(walkroot, dir)
                dstdir = srcdir.replace(state[1], state[2])
                #bb.debug(2, "Staging %s to %s" % (srcdir, dstdir))
                if not dstdir.endswith("/"):
                    dstdir = dstdir + "/"
                shareddirs.append(dstdir)

    # Check the file list for conflicts against files which already exist
    whitelist = (d.getVar("SSTATE_DUPWHITELIST", True) or "").split()
    match = []
    for f in sharedfiles:
        if os.path.exists(f):
            f = os.path.normpath(f)
            realmatch = True
            for w in whitelist:
                if f.startswith(w):
                    realmatch = False
                    break
            if realmatch:
                match.append(f)
                sstate_search_cmd = "grep -rl '%s' %s --exclude=master.list | sed -e 's:^.*/::' -e 's:\.populate-sysroot::'" % (f, d.expand("/home/dam/Projects/FCS/04-Build/build/tmp/sstate-control"))
                search_output = subprocess.Popen(sstate_search_cmd, shell=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE).communicate()[0]
                if search_output != "":
                    match.append("Matched in %s" % search_output.rstrip())
    if match:
        bb.warn("The recipe %s is trying to install files into a shared area when those files already exist. Those files and their manifest location are:\n   %s\nPlease verify which package should provide the above files." % (d.getVar('PN', True), "\n   ".join(match)))

    # Write out the manifest
    f = open(manifest, "w")
    for file in sharedfiles:
        f.write(file + "\n")

    # We want to ensure that directories appear at the end of the manifest
    # so that when we test to see if they should be deleted any contents
    # added by the task will have been removed first.
    dirs = sorted(shareddirs, key=len)
    # Must remove children first, which will have a longer path than the parent
    for di in reversed(dirs):
        f.write(di + "\n")
    f.close()

    # Run the actual file install
    for state in ss['dirs']:
        if os.path.exists(state[1]):
            oe.path.copyhardlinktree(state[1], state[2])

    for postinst in (d.getVar('SSTATEPOSTINSTFUNCS', True) or '').split():
        bb.build.exec_func(postinst, d)

    for lock in locks:
        bb.utils.unlockfile(lock)
}


python do_devshell () {
    if d.getVarFlag("do_devshell", "manualfakeroot"):
       d.prependVar("DEVSHELL", "pseudo ")

            d.appendVar("OE_TERMINAL_EXPORTS", " " + k[0])
       d.delVarFlag("do_devshell", "fakeroot")

}

python gen_packagevar () {
def gen_packagevar(d):
    ret = []
    pkgs = (d.getVar("PACKAGES", True) or "").split()
    vars = (d.getVar("PACKAGEVARS", True) or "").split()
    for p in pkgs:
        for v in vars:
            ret.append(v + "_" + p)

        # Ensure that changes to INCOMPATIBLE_LICENSE re-run do_package for
        # affected recipes.
        ret.append('LICENSE_EXCLUSION-%s' % p)
    return " ".join(ret)
}

python check_conf_exists () {
def check_conf_exists(fn, data):
    bbpath = []
    fn = data.expand(fn)
    vbbpath = data.getVar("BBPATH")
    if vbbpath:
        bbpath += vbbpath.split(":")
    for p in bbpath:
        currname = os.path.join(data.expand(p), fn)
        if os.access(currname, os.R_OK):
            return True
    return False
}
